op_cycle_1� �����Failsafe actions: Stop attempting to move door. Allow normal door movement, but only allow one attempt to move past the suspected mechanical blockage after moving away from it. See retry intervall when a new attempt can be started. Retry Strategy: Every new operation cycle or change in target position If fault is eliminated, re-enable normal operation. Redo calibration during ignition off. NOTE: If failure still exists, stop attempting to move door.�No motor move possible.���Set DTC(s) when door is unable to achieve target feedback voltage. Condition A) A fault is detected if the door is stalled i.e. feedback value has not changed for >(1s) AND the control was not able to reach the intended feedback voltage (within +/-15% hysterisis). Condition B) A fault will also be detected if the control moves the motor for a maximum amount of time (15sec) but is not able to achieve target feedback voltage. For Condition A) If a stalled condition is detected per above description, the module shall execute the following strategy: - After detecting a mechanical block the motor shall back off from the mechanical block for 500ms. - Wait 2 seconds, with motor unpowered - The motor shall then move back to the mechanical block (estimated again 500ms) - The motor shall try to get beyond the previous block (maximum 100msec) - These steps shall be done 8 times. The DTC will log if failure condition is present for more than 24s ((500ms x 2 + 2s) x 8).��- �v  ������ ��  �  � ����Mechanical Failure�ftb_07� ����  � ����� ���������n/a�dtc_9081_fi_0�  �� �      �o@      0@ : �����  � ����� �  8  ����� ��� � ����L� ����@Failsafe actions: Disable circuit. op_cycle_1� �����Mitigation Strategy: Allow normal door movement, but only allow one attempt to move past the suspected mechanical blockage after moving away from it. Retry Strategy: The feedback location where the failure occurs will not be passed for the rest of the key cycle unless the door is able to move in the opposite direction, away from the suspected mechanical blockage. In this case, there will be only 1 attempt to move past the blockage.�No motor move possible.��4Set DTC(s) when door is unable to achieve target feedback voltage. A fault is detected if the door is stalled i.e. feedback value has not changed for >(2s) AND the control was not able to reach the intended feedback voltage (within +/- hysterisis). A fault will also be detected if the control moves the motor for a maximum amount of time (15sec) but is not able to achieve target feedback voltage. If error persists during calibration procedure: calibrated feedback values are not plausible, because door does not move. If a fault is detected per either of the above, the module shall retry to achieve target position every (2 seconds). After (8) consecutive failed attempts the DTC shall be logged and failsafe action(s) taken. The DTC will log if failure condition is present for more than 24s ((500ms x 2 + 2s) x 8).��- �v  ������ ��  �  � ����Mechanical Failure�ftb_07� ����  � ����� ���������n/a�dtc_9082_fi_0�  �� �      �o@      0@ : �����  � ����� �  8  ����� ��� � ����L� ����PMitigation Strategy: Disable circuit for the key cycle (after retry strategy).
